       IDENTIFICATION DIVISION.
       PROGRAM-ID. FDYBIWGA.
       AUTHOR. SYNTHETIC-GEN.
       ENVIRONMENT DIVISION.
       CONFIGURATION SECTION.
       SOURCE-COMPUTER.  SYNTHETIC.
       OBJECT-COMPUTER.  SYNTHETIC.
       DATA DIVISION.
       WORKING-STORAGE SECTION.
       01  OSLCQQ          PIC 9(3).
       01  GBAHYN          PIC 9(5).
       01  UWFOKI          PIC 9(5).
       01  CIOYCS          PIC X(10).
       01  CSRYED          PIC 9(3).
       01  YCCOJG          PIC 9(5).
       01  YNNXUG          PIC 9(3).
       PROCEDURE DIVISION.
       MAIN-PARA.
           ADD CIOYCS TO OSLCQQ.
           ADD OSLCQQ TO GBAHYN.
           MOVE 659 TO UWFOKI.
           ADD YCCOJG TO CIOYCS.
           ADD YCCOJG TO CSRYED.
           MOVE 840 TO YCCOJG.
           ADD CSRYED TO YNNXUG.
           IF YNNXUG > YCCOJG
              DISPLAY "GREATER"
           ELSE
              DISPLAY "NOT-GREATER"
           END-IF.
           MOVE 1 TO ZZYG.
           PERFORM VARYING ZZYG FROM 1 BY 1 UNTIL ZZYG > 5
               PERFORM LOOP-PARA
           END-PERFORM.
           STOP RUN.
